-	script	::CaptainCarocc	-1,{
	if(Class == Job_Novice) {
		cutin "fly_trock",2;
		if(!isbegin_quest(7471)) {
			mes "[Captain Carocc]";
			mes "Had a good dream?";
			mes "Soon, we will get to ^4d4fffIzlude^000000";
			next;
			mes "[Captain Carocc]";
			mes "And you can talk to other people like you just talked to me.";
			next;
			cutin "tutorial01",3;
			mes "!- Information -!";
			mes "^4d4fffLeft mouse click allows basic game controls.";
			mes "Such as conversation with NPC, movement, and attacks.^000000";
			next;
			cutin "fly_trock",2;
			mes "[Captain Carocc]";
			mes "Many youngsters visit the ^4d4fffRune Midgard Kingdom^000000 to chase their dreams.";
			mes "Izlude is a satellite city of Prontera, the capital of the Rune Midgard Kingdom.";
			next;
			mes "[Captain Carocc]";
			mes "Izlude always welcomes young adventurers like you who have just started their journey to the World.";
			mes "You are one of them of course.";
			next;
			mes "[Captain Carocc]";
			mes "I would like to tell you more stories, but it's time to get ready for arrival.";
			mes "There is an academy in Izlude for newcomers like yourself.";
			next;
			mes "[Captain Carocc]";
			mes "Let me give you more details later.";
			mes "See you back at the harbor deck.";
			next;
			mes "[Captain Carocc]";
			mes "To get off this ship, you should enter the ^4d4fffShining Portal^000000 over there.";
			mes "All transportation is made through the portals.";
			setquest 7471;
			completequest 7471;
			close2;
			cutin "",255;
			end;
		}
		mes "[Captain Carocc]";
		mes "Now, we are here in Izlude~";
		mes "Go through that ^4d4fffShining Portal^000000 and exit outside.";
		next;
		mes "[Captain Carocc]";
		mes "Let's talk more when we get off to the deck.";
		mes "There are lots of things I want to teach you.";
		close2;
		cutin "",255;
		end;
	}
}

-	script	::Lumin	-1,{
	if(Class == Job_Novice) {
		if(!isbegin_quest(7471)) {
			mes "[Lumin]";
			mes "............";
			mes "...?";
			next;
			cutin "fly_trock",2;
			mes "[Captain Carocc]";
			mes "Hey, you awake now?";
			mes "That fella without much talk, I rescued him from the ocean.";
			next;
			mes "[Captain Carocc]";
			mes "Think he lost his memory.";
			mes "I gave him a new name 'Lumin'. But, just call him Lu...";
			next;
			mes "[Captain Carocc]";
			mes "And you can talk to other people like you just talked to me.";
			next;
			cutin "tutorial01",3;
			mes "!- Information -!";
			mes "^4d4fffLeft mouse click allows basic game control.";
			mes "Such as conversation with NPC, movement, and attacks.^000000";
			next;
			cutin "fly_trock",2;
			mes "[Captain Carocc]";
			mes "Many youngsters visit the ^4d4fffRune Midgard Kingdom^000000 to chase their dreams.";
			mes "Izlude is a satellite city of Prontera, the capital of the Rune Midgard Kingdom.";
			next;
			mes "[Captain Carocc]";
			mes "Izlude always welcomes young adventurers like you who have just started their journey to the World.";
			mes "You are one of them of course.";
			next;
			mes "[Captain Carocc]";
			mes "I would like to tell you more stories, but it's time to get ready for arrival.";
			mes "There is an academy in Izlude for newcomers like yourself.";
			next;
			mes "[Captain Carocc]";
			mes "Let me give you more detail later.";
			mes "See you back at the harbor deck.";
			next;
			mes "[Captain Carocc]";
			mes "To get off this ship, you should enter the ^4d4fffShining Portal^000000 over there.";
			mes "All transportation is made through those portals.";
			setquest 7471;
			completequest 7471;
			next;
			cutin "nov_lumin01",0;
			mes "[Lumin]";
			mes "Yes.";
			next;
			cutin "fly_trock",2;
			mes "[Carocc]";
			mes "Oh, boy.";
			mes "What cute reaction.";
			close2;
			cutin "",255;
			end;
		}
		cutin "nov_lumin01",0;
		mes "[Lumin]";
		mes ".....";
		next;
		select("Should I introduce myself?:My name is ~!");
		mes "["+strcharinfo(0)+"]";
		mes "I am "+strcharinfo(0)+"!";
		next;
		mes "[Lu]";
		mes ".....";
		next;
		mes "[Lu]";
		mes ".....";
		mes "....So?";
		next;
		mes "- Lu just walked away with a cynical look on his face.";
		next;
		cutin "fly_trock",2;
		mes "[Carocc]";
		mes "He's just shy, you know.";
		mes "You will see him again in Izlude, be good to him please.";
		next;
		mes "[Carocc]";
		mes "From now on, I'll be driving this ship around Izlude.";
		mes "Let's go, shall we?";
		close2;
		cutin "",255;
		end;
	}
}

-	script	::CaptainCaroccIzlude	-1,{
	cutin "fly_trock",2;
	if(Class == Job_Novice && BaseLevel < 15) {
		if(isbegin_quest(4269) == 2) {
			if(!isbegin_quest(7472)) {
				mes "[Carocc]";
				mes "Hmm? You must be a student of the Criatura Academy?";
				mes "Were you on my ship?";
				mes "Hmm I can't remember.";
				next;
				mes "[Carocc]";
				mes "Well, anything is fine.";
				mes "Shall I go easy on you since you said you were a student of the Academy?";
				mes "I am still the captain of the ship, regardless.";
				next;
				mes "[Carocc]";
				mes "I plan on taking off as soon as the repairs are complete.";
				mes "The route will open with ^4d4fffPharos Lighthouse^000000 by then.";
				close2;
				cutin "",255;
				end;
			} else {
				mes "[Carocc]";
				mes "Oh, "+strcharinfo(0)+"!";
				mes "Why are you here at the marina?";
				mes "I guess you are doing well at the academy.";
				next;
				mes "[Carocc]";
				mes "I'm going to be docking and repairing the ship here for a while.";
				mes "I will be taking the same route I tried before.";
				next;
				mes "[Carocc]";
				mes "I plan on taking off as soon as the repairs are complete.";
				mes "The route will open with ^4d4fffPharos Lighthouse^000000 by then.";
				close2;
				cutin "",255;
				end;
			}
		}
		if(isbegin_quest(7471) == 2) {
			if(!isbegin_quest(7472)) {
				mes "[Carocc]";
				mes "This is the city of Izlude.";
				next;
				mes "[Carocc]";
				mes "I know that you're new around here so let me get to the point.";
				next;
				mes "[Carocc]";
				mes "Did you know that there is a new institute of learning for new adventurers?";
				next;
				select("Tell me about it.");
				mes "[Carocc]";
				mes "It's called the ^4d4fffRoyal Criatura Academy.^000000";
				mes "Founded by the Rune Midgard lineage to help out new adventurers.";
				next;
				mes "[Carocc]";
				mes "A friend of mine works there, so I'll introduce you to him.";
				mes "He can show you the ropes around here.";
				next;
				mes "[Carocc]";
				mes "Find him near the north bridge of the city.";
				mes "Go and meet him there.";
				next;
				mes "[Carocc]";
				mes "His name is ^4d4fffHun^000000.";
				mes "I will mark his spot on the map so go to see him.";
				setquest 7472;
				next;
				mes "!- Information -!";
				mes "The ^4d4fffMini map can be seen on the right top of the screen.";
				mes "You can zoom in with +, zoom out with -. The waypoint from the NPC will be marked on it.^000000";
				viewpoint 1,122,207,14,0xFF0000;
				next;
				mes "!- Information -!";
				mes "You received a Quest from ^4d4fffCaptain Carocc.^000000";
				next;
				cutin "tutorial02",3;
				mes "!- Information -!";
				mes "Quest information can be viewed by pressing ^4d4fffAlt + U^000000 key together or by clicking on the ^4d4fffquest button under the Basic Info window.^000000";
				next;
				mes "[Carocc]";
				mes "If you need more help with the map, press "+F_Navi("Hun","izlude,122,207","^4d4fff")+" here.";
				mes "Yes, click on the name 'Hun'.";
				next;
				cutin "navi01",3;
				mes "!- Information -!";
				mes "^4d4fffThe name here is the target^000000 "+F_Navi("Hun","izlude,122,207","^4d4fff");
				next;
				cutin "navi02",3;
				mes "!- Information -!";
				mes "If you press this button, ^4d4fffarrows will point to the location of the objective.^000000";
				next;
				cutin "fly_trock",2;
				mes "[Carocc]";
				mes "Hun will help you register with the academy.";
				mes "I hope it can help you for your future.";
				close2;
				cutin "",255;
				end;
			} else if(isbegin_quest(7472) == 1) {
				mes "[Carocc]";
				mes "If you want, you don't have to go to academy and leave Izlude with the southwest bridge.";
				mes "But, I recommend you visit the Academy first.";
				next;
				mes "[Carocc]";
				mes "The world is a lonely place to be alone.";
				mes "The Academy has people you can make as lifetime companions.";
				next;
				mes "[Carocc]";
				mes "My friend Hun will be around the academy entrance.";
				mes "If you don't know the way I'll point it out to you again.";
				next;
				mes "[Carocc]";
				mes "If you need more help with the map, press "+F_Navi("Hun","izlude,122,207","^4d4fff")+" here.";
				mes "Yes, the part that says 'Hun'.";
				next;
				cutin "navi01",3;
				mes "!- Information -!";
				mes "^4d4fffThe name here is the target^000000 "+F_Navi("Hun","izlude,122,207","^4d4fff");
				next;
				cutin "navi02",3;
				mes "!- Information -!";
				mes "If you press this button, ^4d4fffarrows will point to the location of the objective.^000000";
				next;
				cutin "fly_trock",2;
				mes "[Carocc]";
				mes "Anyway, my friend will help you register with the academy.";
				mes "I hope it will help you out in your journey.";
				close2;
				cutin "",255;
				end;
			} else {
				mes "[Carocc]";
				mes "Oh, "+strcharinfo(0)+"!";
				mes "Still being dilligent?";
				mes "I've been busy, also I was repairing the ship.";
				next;
				mes "[Carocc]";
				mes "I'll be taking off as soon as the repairs are complete.";
				mes "At that time, the sailing route to ^4d4fffPharos Lighthouse^000000 will be opened.";
				mes "Be excited for it.";
				close2;
				cutin "",255;
				end;
			}
		} else {
			if(!isbegin_quest(7472)) {
				mes "[Carocc]";
				mes "Hello?";
				mes "Is it your first time on Izlude?";
				next;
				switch(select("Hello?:Can I board the ship again?:I don't know what to do.")) {
					case 1:
						mes "[Carocc]";
						mes "You look strong and able!";
						mes "I like people like you!";
						mes "Always be healthy and strong as you are now.";
						close2;
						cutin "",255;
						end;
					case 2:
						mes "[Carocc]";
						mes "I usually travel to ^4d4fffPharos Lighthouse.^000000";
						mes "But I'm resting right now due to some problems";
						next;
						mes "[Carocc]";
						mes "If it's Alberta of Byalan Island you want to go to, the sailor will take you there for a small fee.";
						close2;
						cutin "",255;
						end;
					case 3:
						mes "[Carocc]";
						mes "Hmm? You said you didn't know what to do.";
						mes "Since you're at Izlude, why don't you visit ^4d4fffCriatura Academy^000000?";
						next;
						mes "[Carocc]";
						mes "Izlude has a new Institute for budding adventurers like you.";
						mes "A friend of mine works there, so I'll introduce you to him.";
						next;
						mes "[Carocc]";
						mes "He usually talks to new adventurers near the entrance of the academy at the north bridge of Izlude.";
						next;
						if(isbegin_quest(7473)) {
							select("I know who you're talking about.");
							mes "[Carocc]";
							mes "Then there's no worry.";
							mes "He'll introduce you to the academy.";
							next;
							mes "[Carocc]";
							mes "OK. I will give you directions to find him.";
							mes "By the way, did I tell you his name? His name is ^4d4fffHun^000000.";
							next;
							mes "!- Information -!";
							mes "The ^4d4fffMini map can be seen on the top right of the screen.";
							mes "You can zoom in with +, zoom out with -. The waypoint from the NPC will be marked on it.^000000";
							viewpoint 1,122,207,14,0xFF0000;
							next;
							mes "[Carocc]";
							mes "If you need more help with the map, press "+F_Navi("Hun","izlude,122,207","^4d4fff")+" here.";
							mes "Yes, the part that says 'Hun'.";
							next;
							cutin "navi01",3;
							mes "!- Information -!";
							mes "^4d4fffThe name here is the target^000000 "+F_Navi("Hun","izlude,122,207","^4d4fff");
							next;
							cutin "navi02",3;
							mes "!- Information -!";
							mes "If you press this button, ^4d4fffarrows will point to the location of the objective.^000000";
							next;
							cutin "fly_trock",2;
							mes "[Carocc]";
							mes "Anyway, my friend will help you register with the academy.";
							mes "I hope it will help you out in your journey.";
							close2;
							cutin "",255;
							end;
						}
						mes "[Carocc]";
						mes "His name is ^4d4fffHun^000000.";
						mes "I will mark his location on the map so go to see him.";
						setquest 7472;
						next;
						mes "!- Information -!";
						mes "^4d4fffMini map can be seen on the right top of the screen.";
						mes "You can zoom in with +, zoom out with -. The waypoint from the NPC will be marked on it.^000000";
						viewpoint 1,122,207,14,0xFF0000;
						next;
						mes "!- Information -!";
						mes "Received a Quest from ^4d4fffCaptain Carocc.";
						mes "Contents of your Quest can be monitored on the Quest information window.^000000";
						next;
						cutin "tutorial02",3;
						mes "!- Information -!";
						mes "Quest window can be opened by pressing ^4d4fffAlt + U^000000 key.";
						next;
						mes "[Carocc]";
						mes "If you need more help with the map, press "+F_Navi("Hun","izlude,122,207","^4d4fff")+" here.";
						mes "Yes, the part that says 'Hun'.";
						next;
						cutin "navi01",3;
						mes "!- Information -!";
						mes "^4d4fffThe name here is the target^000000 "+F_Navi("Hun","izlude,122,207","^4d4fff");
						next;
						cutin "navi02",3;
						mes "!- Information -!";
						mes "If you press this button, ^4d4fffarrows will point to the location of the objective.^000000";
						next;
						cutin "fly_trock",2;
						mes "[Carocc]";
						mes "Anyway, my friend will help you register with the academy.";
						mes "I hope it will help you out in your journey.";
						close2;
						cutin "",255;
						end;
				}
			} else if(isbegin_quest(7472) == 1) {
				mes "[Carocc]";
				mes "Ah, it's you.";
				mes "This guy has also decided to register at Criatura Academy.";
				mes "Maybe you can help each other out and become friends.";
				next;
				cutin "nov_lumin01",0;
				mes "[Lumin]";
				mes "....";
				next;
				cutin "fly_trock",2;
				mes "[Carocc]";
				mes "I recommend you visit Academy first.";
				next;
				mes "[Carocc]";
				mes "The world is a lonely place to be alone.";
				mes "The Academy has people you could make into lifetime companions.";
				next;
				mes "[Carocc]";
				mes "My friend "+F_Navi("Hun","izlude,122,207","^4d4fff")+" will be around the academy entrance at the northern bridge.";
				mes "If you don't know the way I'll point it out to you again.";
				next;
				mes "[Carocc]";
				mes "Then, good luck!";
				close2;
				cutin "",255;
				end;
			} else {
				mes "[Carocc]";
				mes "Oh, We meet again.";
				mes "Do you by any chance need a ship?";
				mes "I usually travel to Pharos Lighthouse but I'm stuck here gathering supplies.";
				mes "If you need to go to Pharos later, come see me.";
				close2;
				cutin "",255;
				end;
			}
		}
	} else {
		if(isbegin_quest(7472) == 2) {
			mes "[Carocc]";
			mes "It's been a while.";
			mes "Looking at your expression, you must be doing well.";
			next;
			switch(select("Take me to Pharos Lighthouse:To Alberta:Talk")) {
				case 1:
					mes "[Carocc]";
					mes "Do you want to go to Pharos Lighthouse on the southern coast of Morocc?";
					mes "The fee is 2800 zeny. I have a crew that needs payment so this fee is non-negotiable.";
					next;
					if(select("To Pharos Lighthouse~:Cancel.") == 2) {
						mes "[Carocc]";
						mes "OK.";
						mes "Do you know this, by the way?";
						mes "^4d4fffThere's Rogue hideout at Pharos Lighthouse.^000000";
						mes "You already knew this?";
						close2;
						cutin "",255;
						end;
					}
					if(Zeny < 2800) {
						mes "[Carocc]";
						mes "Sorry but you are short of the boarding fee.";
						mes "You need 2800 zeny to travel.";
						close2;
						cutin "",255;
						end;
					}
					mes "[Carocc]";
					mes "Let us travel with the wind in our hair.";
					set Zeny,Zeny-2800;
					close2;
					warp "cmd_fild07",92,129;
					end;
				case 2:
					mes "[Carocc]";
					mes "I thought you knew that I only go to Pharos.";
					mes "Ask the sailor over there, he's the one that goes there frequently.";
					next;
					mes "[Carocc]";
					mes "There are plenty of other ships that travel to Alberta and Byalan Islands.";
					close2;
					cutin "",255;
					end;
				case 3:
					mes "[Carocc]";
					mes "Hmm. I'm content with the wellbing of you and other adventurers who passed me by.";
					next;
					mes "[Carocc]";
					mes "Lumin mus be doing well, too.";
					mes "I wonder why you feel like my own child even though we've only met from the sea.";
					close2;
					cutin "",255;
					end;
			}
		}
		mes "[Carocc]";
		mes "I am  Carocc, the captain of this ship.";
		mes "Do you need a ship?";
		next;
		if(select("Pharos Lighthouse - 2800z:Don't need it") == 2) {
			mes "[Carocc]";
			mes "Then use it next time.";
			close2;
			cutin "",255;
			end;
		}
		if(Zeny < 2800) {
			mes "[Carocc]";
			mes "Sorry but you are short of the boarding fee.";
			mes "I need 2800z to operate.";
			close2;
			cutin "",255;
			end;
		}
		mes "[Carocc]";
		mes "Let us travel with the wind in our hairs.";
		set Zeny,Zeny-2800;
		close2;
		warp "cmd_fild07",92,129;
		end;
	}

OnTouch:
	if(Class == Job_Novice && BaseLevel < 15 && !isbegin_quest(4269))
		emotion e_gasp;
	else
		emotion e_heh;	
	end;
OnInit:
	questinfo 7472,QTYPE_QUEST,1,Job_Novice;
	setquestinfo_level 7472,1,14;
	setquestinfo_req 7472,7473,0;
	end;
}

-	script	::IncreaseAgiAco	-1,{
	mes "[Acolyte]";
	mes "Welcome welcome! I know you Criatura students need a lot of energy to get to your classes on time.";
	next;
	mes "[Acolyte]";
	mes "If you want to get around more quickly I can cast [^4d4fffIncrease Agi^000000] on you.";
	mes "It'll just last for a few minutes but it'll really useful for getting around.";
	next;
	if(select("Yes, please:No, thank you.") == 2) {
		mes "[Acolyte]";
		mes "Sure, come back anytime you need a lift!";
		close;
	}
	mes "[Acolyte]";
	mes "Sure, here you go! Don't forget, be nice when asking for buffs from Acolytes and Priests!";
	npcskill "AL_INCAGI",10,99,60;
	close;

				case 4:

					mes "If you'd like to go on a honeymoon to ^8B4513Jawaii^000000, the paradise of newlyweds, please speak to the "+F_Navi("Newlywed Helper",.@map$+",180,224","^B9062F")+".";
					mes "Would you like to check any other locations?";
					viewpoint 1,180,224,11,0xFF0000;
					next;
					break;
				case 5:
					callsub L_Mark, F_Navi("Mercenary Guildsman",.@map$+",47,170","^0000FF");
					viewpoint 1,47,170,12,0xDA70D6;
					next;
					break;
				case 6:
					callsub L_Mark, F_Navi("Pet Groomer","izlude_in,72,98"),1;
					viewpoint 1,108,179,13,0x006400;
					next;
					break;
				case 7:
					set .@loop,0;
					break;
				}
			}
			break;
		case 3:
			mes "[Information Staff]";
			mes "Sure, I'll remove all marks from your mini-map.";
			mes "Is there anything else I can do for you?";
			viewpoint 2,1,1,0,0xFFFF00;
			viewpoint 2,1,1,1,0x000000;
			viewpoint 2,1,1,2,0xFF0000;
			viewpoint 2,1,1,3,0xFFFF00;
			viewpoint 2,1,1,4,0xFFFF00;
			viewpoint 2,1,1,5,0xFFFF00;
			viewpoint 2,1,1,6,0xFFFF00;
			viewpoint 2,1,1,7,0xFFFF00;
			viewpoint 2,1,1,8,0xFFFF00;
			viewpoint 2,1,1,9,0xFFFF00;
			viewpoint 2,1,1,10,0xFFFF00;
			viewpoint 2,1,1,11,0xFFFF00;
			viewpoint 2,1,1,12,0xFFFF00;
			viewpoint 2,1,1,13,0xFFFF00;
			next;
			break;
		case 4:
			mes "[Information Staff]";
			mes "Enjoy your stay.";
			mes "Bye~!";
			close;
		}
	}
	end;

L_Mark:
	mes "[Information Staff]";
	if(getarg(1,0)) {
		mes "Let me mark the location of the";
		mes getarg(0);
	} else
		mes "Let me mark the location of the "+getarg(0);
	mes "on your mini-map.";
	mes "Would you like to check any other locations?";
	return;
OnInit:
	questinfo 7474,QTYPE_QUEST,1;
	setquestinfo_level 7474,1,14;
	end;
}

				close;
			}
			if(getequipid(EQI_ARMOR) != 2302) {
				mes "[Almond J]";
				mes "Hmm, wait you should be equipped with your cotton shirt.";
				close;
			}
			mes "[Almond J]";
			mes "Now!! Start the first hidden enchant!! Start!!!!!";
			next;
			specialeffect2 EF_REPAIRWEAPON;
			progressbar "ffff00",2;
			mes "[Almond J]";
			mes "Zzazanzn!! Completed!!";

		mes "How about it? Don't you think the hidden enchant is great? Any chance to do another hidden enchant?";
		next;
		mes "[Almond J]";
		mes "It's fun. I want to do it again.";
		mes "Hey, another trial ok? Aaaaa!!! I want to do the hidden enchant again.";
		next;

		close;
	}

izlude,153,126,1	duplicate(RefineryOwnerHan)	Refinery Owner Han#iz	4_M_02
izlude_a,153,126,1	duplicate(RefineryOwnerHan)	Refinery Owner Han#iz_a	4_M_02
izlude_b,153,126,1	duplicate(RefineryOwnerHan)	Refinery Owner Han#iz_b	4_M_02

-	script	::RefiningMachineWagjak	-1,{
	disable_items;
	mes "[Refining Machine Wagjak]";
	mes "- Ddarritt! -";
	mes "Wagjak Starting... Completed..";
	mes "Checking the user.. Completed.";
	mes "Select the refining equipment.";
	next;
	setarray .@position$[1],"Head","Body","Left hand","Right hand","Robe","Shoes","Accessory 1","Accessory 2","Head 2","Head 3";
	set .@menu$,"";
	for(set .@i,1; .@i<=10; set .@i,.@i+1)
		set .@menu$,.@menu$+(getequipisequiped(.@i)?getequipname(.@i):.@position$[.@i]+"-[Unarmed]")+":";
	set .@part,select(.@menu$);
	if(!getequipisequiped(.@part)) {
		mes "[Refining Machine Wagjak]";
		mes "^ff0000- Error number 000"+.@part+" -^000000";
		mes "Item is not equipped.";
		close;
	}
	mes "[Refining Machine Wagjak]";
	mes "Searching for the equipment information - completed.";
	next;
	if(!getequipisenableref(.@part)) {
		mes "[Refining Machine Wagjak]";
		mes "^ff0000- Error number 000"+.@part+"1 -^000000";
		mes "This equipment is impossible to refine.";
		close;
	}
	if(getequiprefinerycnt(.@part) >= 10) {
		mes "[Refining Machine Wagjak]";
		mes "^FF0000- Error number 1010 -^000000";
		mes "At the current version, you can do refining up to level 10.";
		close;
	}
	set .@refineitemid, getequipid(.@part);
	set .@refinerycnt, getequiprefinerycnt(.@part);
	switch(getequipweaponlv(.@part)) {
		case 0: //Armor
			set .@type$,"Armor";
			set .@material,985; //Elunium
			set .@price,2000;
			set .@safe,4;
			break;
		case 1: //Level 1 weapon
			set .@type$,"Level 1 weapon";
			set .@material,1010; //Phracon
			set .@price,50;
			set .@safe,7;
			break;
		case 2: //Level 2 weapon
			set .@type$,"Level 2 weapon";
			set .@material,1011; //Emveretarcon
			set .@price,200;
			set .@safe,6;
			break;
		case 3: //Level 3 weapon
			set .@type$,"Level 3 weapon";
			set .@material,984; //Oridecon
			set .@price,5000;
			set .@safe,5;
			break;
		case 4: //Level 4 weapon
			set .@type$,"Level 4 weapon";
			set .@material,984; //Oridecon
			set .@price,20000;
			set .@safe,4;
			break;
		case 5: //Other
			set .@type$,"Other";
			set .@material,985; //Elunium
			set .@price,2000;
			set .@safe,4;
			break;
	}
	set .@count,1;
	if(VIP_SCRIPT && !vip_status(1)) {
		switch(getequipweaponlv(.@part)) {
			case 0: set .@price,.@price * 10; break;
			case 1: set .@price,.@price * 40; break;
			case 2: set .@price,.@price * 50; break;
			case 3: set .@price,.@price * 2; break;
			case 4: set .@price,.@price * 2; break;
			case 5: set .@price,.@price * 10; break;
		}
	}
	mes "[Refining Machine Wagjak]";
	mes "Type : "+.@type$;
	mes "Charge : "+getitemname(.@material)+", "+(.@price>=10000?callfunc("F_InsertComma",.@price,3):.@price)+" zeny.";
	if(isbegin_quest(5153) == 1 && getequipweaponlv(.@part) == 1) {
		mes "Service usage coupon sensed. No charge to be requested. Will you refine?";
		set .@price,0;
		set .@count,0;
	} else
		mes "Above money will be charged. Will you refine?";
	next;
	if(select("Refine.:Don't refine.") == 2) {
		mes "[Refining Machine Wagjak]";
		mes "Cancel the refining.";
		close;
	}
	if(getequippercentrefinery(.@part) < 100) {
		mes "[Refining Machine Wagjak]";
		mes "- Ddarritt! -";
		mes "The user's confirmation required.";
		mes "You are attempting unsafe refining.";
		mes "If refining fails, the equipment will be destroyed. Will you continue?";
		next;
		if(select("Refine.:Don't refine.") == 2) {
			mes "[Refining Machine Wagjak]";
			mes "Refining has been cancelled as per the user's request.";
			close;
		}
	}
	if(countitem(.@material) < .@count || Zeny < .@price) {
		mes "[Refining Machine Wagjak]";
		mes "^ff0000- Error number 8282 -^000000";
		mes "You are short of refining price or "+getitemname(.@material)+".";
		close;
	}
	set Zeny,Zeny-.@price;
	delitem .@material,.@count;
	//anti-hack
	if(callfunc("F_IsEquipIDHack",.@part,.@refineitemid) ||
		callfunc("F_IsEquipRefineHack",.@part,.@refinerycnt)) {
		mes "[Refining Machine Wagjak]";
		mes "^ff0000- Error number 666 -^000000";
		mes "The equipment has been switched.";
		close;
	}
	if(getequippercentrefinery(.@part) <= rand(100)) {
		failedrefitem .@part;
		mes "[Refining Machine Wagjak]";
		mes "Result : Fail";
		mes "Refining failed. The equipment was destroyed.";
		close;
	}
	successrefitem .@part;
	mes "[Refining Machine Wagjak]";
	mes "Result : Success";
	mes "Congratulations!! You succeeded in refining.";
	if(!.@price && !.@count) {
		completequest 5153;
		next;
		mes "[Refining Machine Wagjak]";
		mes "Service usage coupon was used.";
	}
	close;
}

izlude_a,153,121,3	duplicate(RefiningMachineWagjak)	Refining Machine Wagjak::iz_a	2_MONEMUS
izlude_b,153,121,3	duplicate(RefiningMachineWagjak)	Refining Machine Wagjak::iz_b	2_MONEMUS

		mes "Welcome. The owner told me to explain to you about ^4d4fffthe weapon levels^000000 and ^4d4fffsafety refining.^000000";
		next;
		mes "[Tadde]";
		mes "In fact, it is better to get to know while questing yourself. But anyway if you have any questions, please ask to me.";
		next;
		set .@menu,3;
	} else {
		mes "[Tadde]";
		mes "I am selling the metal for refining weapons made of iron or carbon steel.";
		mes "I am selling ^007777Phracon^000000 for refining level 1 weapons and ^007777Emveretarcon^000000 for refining level 2 weapons as much as possible.";
		next;
		set .@menu,select("Phracon - 200z:Emveretarcon - 1000z:Other questions...");
	}
	switch(.@menu) {
		case 1:
			mes "[Tadde]";
			mes "How many pieces of ^007777Phracon^000000 are you going to buy? To stop buying, input 0.";
			next;
			while(1) {
				input .@input;
				if(!.@input) {
					mes "[Tadde]";
					mes "Trade has been cancelled.";
					close;
				} else if(.@input < 0 || .@input > 500) {
					mes "[Tadde]";
					mes "Tell me how many you want under 500 pieces";
					next;
				} else
					break;
			}
			set .@sell,.@input*1000;
			if(Zeny < .@sell) {
				mes "[Tadde]";
				mes "I am sorry but you are short of money. I can't give you these free of charge.";
				close;
			}
			getitem 1010,.@input; //Phracon
			set Zeny, Zeny-.@sell;
			mes "[Tadde]";
			mes "Thank you for purchsae.";
			close;
		case 2:
			mes "[Tadde]";
			mes "How many pieces of ^007777Emveretarcon^000000 are you going to buy? To stop buying, input 0.";
			next;
			while(1) {
				input .@input;
				if(!.@input) {
					mes "[Tadde]";
					mes "Trade has been cancelled.";
					close;
				} else if(.@input < 0 || .@input > 500) {
					mes "[Tadde]";
					mes "Tell me how many you want under 500 pieces";
					next;
				} else
					break;
			}
			set .@sell,.@input*1000;
			if(Zeny < .@sell) {
				mes "[Tadde]";
				mes "I am sorry but you are short of money. I can't give you these free of charge.";
				close;
			}
			getitem 1011,.@input; //Emveretarcon
			set Zeny, Zeny-.@sell;
			mes "[Tadde]";
			mes "Thank you for purchsae.";
			close;
		case 3:
			if(isbegin_quest(5154) != 1) {
				mes "[Tadde]";
				mes "Any questions about the weapon level and safety refining?";
				next;
			}
			while(1) {
				switch(select("Weapon level:Safety refining:"+(isbegin_quest(5154)==1?"Finish the question":"End coversation")+".")) {
					case 1:
						mes "[Tadde]";
						mes "Weapons have level, where as Armors don't. The more ^4d4fffupscaled a weapon^000000 is, the higher the weapon level is.";
						next;
						mes "[Tadde]";
						if(isbegin_quest(5154) == 1)
							mes "That means ^b9062fthe upscaled weapons are more difficult to obtain..^000000";
						else
							mes "It means the upscaled weapons are more difficult to obtain.";
						next;
						mes "[Tadde]";
						mes "Considering the customers coming for refining, the ones for refining level 1&2 weapons are more than those for level 3&4 weapons.";
						next;
						break;
					case 2:
						mes "[Tadde]";

							mes "Safety refining differs from the levels of Armor or Weapon, so basically each level has a ^4d4fffdifferent safe upgrade level.^000000";
						else
							mes "Safety refining differs from the levels of Armor or Weapon, it refers to the level that is safe from breaking while refining.";
						next;
						while(1) {
							switch(select("Level 1 weapon:Level 2 weapon:Level 3 weapon:Level 4 weapon:Armor:Question finished")) {
								case 1:
									mes "[Tadde]";
									mes "Level 1 weapons are safe when refined up to ^b9062f+7^000000. The lower the level of weapon is, the higher the figure of the refining is possible.";
									next;
									mes "[Tadde]";
									mes "But the effect is minimal.";
									next;
									break;
								case 2:
									mes "[Tadde]";
									mes "Level 2 weapons are safe when refined up to ^b9062f+6^000000, even though refining figure is lower than level 1 weapon.";
									next;
									mes "[Tadde]";
									mes "Of course, it has stronger effect than level 1 weapon.";
									next;
									break;
								case 3:
									mes "[Tadde]";
									mes "Level 3 weapons are safe when refined up to ^b9062f+5^000000. Simply speaking, it looks like the safety refining goes down by 1 according to each weapon level.";
									next;
									mes "[Tadde]";
									mes "The higher the weapon is, the increasing effect of +1 becomes higher as well";
									next;
									break;
								case 4:
									mes "[Tadde]";
									mes "Level 4 weapons are safe up to ^b9062f+4^000000. Numbers of level 4 weapons are so rare that not so many customers bring them here.";
									next;
									mes "[Tadde]";
									mes "As it is one of the most luxurious weapons, the effect of refining is the strongest.";
									next;
									break;
								case 5:
									mes "[Tadde]";
									mes "Armors are safe when refined up to ^b9062f+4^000000, just like a level 4 weapon.";
									next;
									mes "[Tadde]";
									mes "As most refiners are used to making weapons it's hard for them to safely upgrade armors.";
									next;
									break;
								case 6:
									mes "[Tadde]";
									mes "You look like you've had enough explanations about the safety refining.";
									next;
									set .@end,1;
									break;
							}
							if(.@end)
								break;
						}
						break;
					case 3:

	}

-	script	::RepairMan	-1,{
	mes "[Repair Man]";
	mes "Repairing broken equipment!! if you have a broken equipment, bring it to me anytime.";
	next;
	switch(select("Repair it.:Nothing to be repaired now.:What is repairing?")) {
		case 1:
			set .@repairprice,5000;
			set .@checkitem,1;
			while(1) {
				if(!getbrokenid(.@checkitem))
					break;
				set .@checkitem,.@checkitem+1;
			}
			set .@checkitem,.@checkitem-1;
			if(!.@checkitem) {
				mes "[Repair Man]";
				mes "You may treat the equipments carefully... As you don't have nothing to be repaired.";
				close;
			}
			mes "[Repair Man]";
			mes "Hmmm... let's see... oh.. hmm...";
			next;
			set .@totalcost,.@repairprice*.@checkitem;
			mes "[Repair Man]";
			mes "------------------------";
			mes "Damaged Equipment Estimate";
			mes "Damaged Equipment: ^FF0000"+.@checkitem+"?000000";
			mes "Fee: ^0000FF"+.@totalcost+" Zeny^000000";
			mes "------------------------";
			mes "Would you like to proceed with the repair?";
			next;
			switch(select("Yes:No")) {
				case 1:
					if(Zeny < .@totalcost) {
						mes "[Repair Man]";
						mes "The repair cost is "+.@repairprice+" Zeny per damaged equipment. You do not have enough money.";
						close;
					}
					set .@checkitem2,1;
					while(1) {
						if(!getbrokenid(.@checkitem2))
							break;
						set .@checkitem2,.@checkitem2+1;
					}
					set .@checkitem2,.@checkitem2-1;
					if(.@checkitem == .@checkitem2) {
						set Zeny, Zeny-.@totalcost;
						while(.@checkitem) {
							repair(.@checkitem);
							set .@checkitem,.@checkitem-1;
						}
						mes "[Repair Man]";
						mes "The repair has been completed. Be sure to take good care of your equipment.";
						close;
					} else {
						mes "[Repair Man]";
						mes "Mmm? Something's wrong. Wait... Equip the items you need to repair and then come back to me.";
						close;
					}
				case 2:
					mes "[Repair Man]";
					mes "Well, I don't care. After all, it's not my equipment. However, leaving equipment unchecked is not a wise choice.";
					close;
			}
		case 2:
			mes "[Repair Man]";
			mes "If you don't have eny equipments to be repaired, you may not have something to talk with me.";
			close;
		case 3:
			mes "[Repair Man]";
			mes "A specific skill or boss monster could break your equipments frequently.";
			next;
			mes "[Repair Man]";
			mes "This doesn't maean that your equipment is gone forever like what happens during refining.";
			next;
			mes "[Repair Man]";
			mes "When your item breaks this way, they won't perform normally...";
			next;
			mes "[Repair Man]";
			mes "In this case, bring it to me, and I will repair it back to new at the cost of 5000 zeny for each equipment.";
			close;
	}
}

-	script	::AcademyReceptionist	-1,{
	if(isbegin_quest(7117) == 1) { erasequest 7117; }
	if(isbegin_quest(7118) == 1) { erasequest 7118; }
	if(isbegin_quest(7119) == 1) { erasequest 7119; }
	if(isbegin_quest(7120) == 1) { erasequest 7120; }
	if(isbegin_quest(7121) == 1) { erasequest 7121; }
	if(isbegin_quest(7122) == 1) { erasequest 7122; }
	if(isbegin_quest(7123) == 1) { erasequest 7123; }
	if(isbegin_quest(7124) == 1) { erasequest 7124; }
	if(isbegin_quest(7126) == 1) { erasequest 7126; }
	if(isbegin_quest(7127) == 1) { erasequest 7127; }
	if(isbegin_quest(4269) == 2) {
		mes "[Receptionist]";
		mes "Hello, "+strcharinfo(0)+".";
		mes "How are you today?";
		mes "I am in charge guiding you here in the Academy.";
		next;
	} else {
		mes "[Receptionist]";
		mes "Welcome to our Academy. I am in charge with the guide and registration for Novice education courses.";
		next;
	}
	while(1) {
		mes "[Receptionist]";
		mes "What can I do for you?";
		next;
		if(isbegin_quest(4269) == 2)
			set .@menu$,":What's inside and outside the Academy.:Trainer location guide.:End Coversation.";
		else
			set .@menu$,"Register for the Academy:Explanation about the Academy:Location for trainers:Coversation finished";
		switch(select(.@menu$)) {
			case 1:
				if(Class == Job_Novice) {
					if(!isbegin_quest(60457))
						setquest 60457;
					if(!checkweight(1201,1) || (MaxWeight - Weight) < 2000) {
						mes "- As you are overloaded with too many items, quest can't be continued.";
						close;
					}
					mes "[Receptionist]";
					mes "Let me see... Your name is... "+strcharinfo(0)+".";
					mes "I will make a new registration for you.";
					mes "You can choose the course freely and each course has individual features.";
					next;
					mes "[Receptionist]";
					mes "And this is the basic equipment for the educational course.";
					mes "Please make a good use of it.";
					mes "Be careful with it as it won't be provided again.";
					setquest 4269;
					completequest 4269;
					setquest 11255;
					getitem 2352,1; //Novice_Plate
					getitem 2510,1; //Novice_Hood
					getitem 2414,1; //Novice_Boots
					getitem 5055,1; //Novice_Egg_Cap
					getitem 1243,1; //Novice_Knife
					getitem 2112,1; //Novice_Guard
					getitem 18730,1; //Criatura_Academy_Hat
					getitem 6593,1; //Criatura_Hair_Coupon
					getitem 569,300; //Novice_Potion
					next;
					mes "[Receptionist]";
					mes "It is your first step to be an adventurer that you have made a visit to us.";
					getexp 100,100;
					next;
					mes "[Receptionist]";
					mes "On our next meeting, I anticipate you will grow up a bit more.";
					close;
				} else {
					mes "[Receptionist]";
					mes "One who is not a Novice can't attend the educational course.";
					next;
					mes "[Receptionist]";
					mes "However, a part of the educational course except the character cultivation can be freely attended.";
					mes "So, you may look around the Academy and neighbouring places.";
					if(!isbegin_quest(60457))
						setquest 60457;
					close;
				}
			case 2:

			}
			close;
		case 2:
			if(!countitem(6593)) {
				mes "[Otter Samssoon]";
				mes "Come on.. Honey~";
				mes "You should bring ^ff0000'Criatura Hair Coupon'^000000 for changing hair...";
				close;
			}
			mes "[Otter Samssoon]";
			mes "Honey~ What style do you want?";
			mes "You are totally my style. So I am very excited~~";
			mes "Pick the style from page 1 to 19.";
			next;
			input .@style;
			if(.@style > 19) {
				mes "[Otter Samssoon]";
				mes "Come on.. Honey~ You can use a coupon for the hair style in here~";
				close;
			} else if(!.@style) {
				mes "[Otter Samssoon]";
				mes "Oh my!!? You do not want to?";
				close;
			} else if(getlook(1) == .@style) {
				mes "[Otter Samssoon]";
				mes "Come on.. Honey~ That is the same style you have.";
				mes "Do you want to try something new?";
				close;
			}
			callsub L_cutin,.@style;
			mes "[Otter Samssoon]";
			mes "Style ("+.@style+")?";
			mes "It feels like this.. How is it?";
			next;
			if(select("Good.:No.") == 1) {
				if(!getlook(6)) {
					mes "[Otter Samssoon]";
					mes "Right!";
					mes "Honey! What about dying hair as well?";
					mes "Dying hair also included in this service.";
					next;
					switch(select("Passionate Red:Sweet Yellow:Fatal Purple:Glamourous Orange:Comfortable Green:Clear Blue:Transparent White:Dark Black:Stop.")) {
						case 1:
							set .@pallete,8;
							break;
						case 2:
							set .@pallete,1;
							break;
						case 3:
							set .@pallete,2;
							break;
						case 4:
							set .@pallete,3;
							break;
						case 5:
							set .@pallete,4;
							break;
						case 6:
							set .@pallete,5;
							break;
						case 7:
							set .@pallete,6;
							break;
						case 8:
							set .@pallete,7;
							break;
						case 9:
							mes "[Otter Samssoon]";
							mes "No?";
							mes "Do you need more time? If you want to keep the same color, then select the same one.";
							close2;
							cutin "",255;
							end;
					}
				}
				nude;
				mes "[Otter Samssoon]";
				mes "Relax, it is almost done~";
				next;
				mes "[Otter Samssoon]";
				mes "- Sha sha shak shak shak -";
				mes "- Chikak, crack, crack.. -";
				mes "- Snap, snap, snap.. Crack -";
				next;
				delitem 6593,1;	//Criatura_Hair_Coupon
				if(isbegin_quest(11255) == 1)
					completequest 11255;
				cutin "",255;
				mes "[Otter Samssoon]";
				mes "Oh my! Oh my! Oh my!";
				mes "This hair style no.("+.@style+") suits to you looks good~";
				mes "What do you think?";
				setlook 1,.@style;
				setlook 6,.@pallete;
				next;
				mes "[Otter Samssoon]";
				mes "I want to take care of your style..";
				mes "But I have no choice to select customers because I belong to here.";
				next;
				mes "[Otter Samssoon]";
				mes "For changing to new style, ^ff0000Alberta or Lighthalzen^000000.";
				mes "For dying hair, ^ff0000Prontera or Lighthalzen^000000.";
				close;
			}
			mes "[Otter Samssoon]";
			mes "Honey~ You don't like it?";
			mes "Ahem.. Do you want to read style book again?";
			mes "Take your time and tell me when you decide~ Okay?~";
			close;
		case 3:
			mes "[Otter Samssoon]";
			mes "You can receive ^ff0000criatura hair coupon^000000 from ^ff0000academy receptionist for novice at academy front desk or eden group^000000";
			next;
			mes "[Otter Samssoon]";
			mes "They don't give you for free.. Well..";
			mes "The equipment you had received when you arrived at academy?";
			mes "They change ^ff0000egg shell for novice^000000 to coupon?";
			next;
			mes "[Otter Samssoon]";
			mes "This service has started since I came here. So.. No free service if you have no coupon~";
			close;
		case 4:
			mes "[Otter Samssoon]";
			mes "Oh my!!? Honey, you are not going to change hair?";
			mes "You look nice now rough style.";
			close;
	}

L_cutin:
	if(Sex) {
		if(getarg(0) < 10)
			cutin "hair_m_0"+getarg(0),4;
		else
			cutin "hair_m_"+getarg(0),4;
	} else {
		if(getarg(0) < 10)
			cutin "hair_f_0"+getarg(0),4;
		else
			cutin "hair_f_"+getarg(0),4;
	}
	return;
}

						break;
					case 5:

			}
		}
	} else {
		mes "[Mainz]";

		close;
	}
	end;

	emotion e_otl;
	end;

					cutin "",3;

						mes "We'll cook it right away when you bring the ingredients.";
					else
						mes "When you bring all the ingredients we'll make them for you.";

					close2;
					set ac_cooking_back,1;
					setquest 14157;
					end;
			}
		}

		mes "[Dacquoise]";

		mes "You must be attracted by him.";
		close;
	}

			next;
			mes "[Battle Instructor Subino]";
		} else
			mes getarg(5)+" "+getarg(6)+" at the ^ff0000West field of Izlude^000000.";
		mes getarg(7)+" ^ff0000"+(getarg(0)==11344?"5":"10")+" "+getarg(5)+"s^000000 and bring ^ff0000"+getarg(4)+" "+getarg(8)+"^000000.";
		mes "You can check received quests by pressing ^ff0000Alt + U^000000.";

							mes "[Attribute Expert]";
							mes "How much damage did you give?";
							next;
							input .@input,1,100000;
							if(.@input < 10) {
								mes "[Attribute Expert]";
								mes "Oh man, "+.@input+"! Are you even trying?";
								mes "You're barely hitting it.";
							} else if(.@input > 9 && .@input < 100001) {
								mes "[Attribute Expert]";
								mes "You are good I guess...";
							} else {
								mes "[Attribute Expert]";
								mes "But wait that's impossible.";
								close;
							}
							next;
							mes "[Attribute Expert]";
							mes "All right. Class is over.";
							next;
							mes "[Attribute Expert]";
							mes "I am not sure if you remember monsters with ^ff0000Fire^000000 are weak against ^4d4fffWater^000000.";
							next;
							mes "[Attribute Expert]";
							mes "I will give the ^4d4fffWater^000000 attribute to you as a present.";
							mes "If you attack the Fire Eggs again you should do more damage now.";
							next;
							mes "[Attribute Expert]";
							mes "There is only one more chance!";
							mes "Hurry up, the attribute magic will be gone if you take more time thanks for joining to my class.";
							completequest 2299;
							if(Class == Job_Novice)
								getexp 100,20;
							skilleffect "ITEM_ENCHANTARMS",0;
							sc_start2 SC_ENCHANTARMS,90000,2,1;
							close;
						case 2:
							mes "[Attribute Expert]";
							mes "Go and smack those eggs over there.";
							mes "The egg of an ant is strong so don't worry about destroying them too much.";
							close;
						case 3:
							mes "[Attribute Expert]";
							mes "There is nothing I can do. But I will help you anytime if you meed.";
							erasequest 2299;
							close;
					}
				} else {
					mes "[Attribute Expert]";
					mes "Magic basically consists of different attribute attacks. There is another way of giving the attribute to your weapon by using skill or item. You will learn more the longer you play. Good luck!";
					close;
				}
			case 4:
				mes "[Attribute Expert]";
				mes "Are you getting interested in the depth of the different attributes?";
				close;
		}
	}

OnInit:
	questinfo 2299,QTYPE_QUEST,0;
	end;
}

function	script	F_PetInformation	{
	switch(select("Taming a monster:Hatching "+(getarg(0)?"an":"the")+" egg:Monitoring pet's status:Feeding:Performances:Removing the accessory:Transforming back to egg:End Conversation")) {
		case 1:
			mes "[Adept Adventurer]";
			mes "Only some monsters can become pets and they all have different things to tame them.";
			next;
			mes "[Adept Adventurer]";
			mes "Each monster that can be tamed requires a specific ^4d4ffftaming item^000000.";
			next;
			cutin "pet_ex_01",3;
			mes "[Adept Adventurer]";
			mes "To begin taming, ^4d4fffdouble click^000000 the taming item in your inventory and select which monster to tame.";
			next;
			cutin "pet_ex_02",3;
			mes "[Adept Adventurer]";
			mes "Press ^4d4fffClick^000000 in the center of the pop-up slot machine to tame the monster..";
			next;
			mes "[Adept Adventurer]";
			mes "If successful, the monster will be transformed into an egg!";
			cutin "",255;
			next;
			break;
		case 2:
			mes "[Adept Adventurer]";
			mes "Hatching requires you to have a ^4d4fff<Pet Incubator>^000000 to awaken a monster in the egg.";
			next;
			mes "[Adept Adventurer]";
			mes "Most towns have a ^4d4fff<Pet Groomer>^000000 where you can but the ^4d4fff<Pet Incubator>^000000.";
			mes "Ask the town guide for the location of the Pet Groomer if you can't find them.";
			next;
			break;
		case 3:
			mes "[Adept Adventurer]";
			mes "^4d4fffRight-click^000000 on your pet and select ^4d4fffCheck the Pet Status^000000 to check on its status.";
			mes "Or you can press ^4d4fff<Alt + J>^000000.";
			next;
			mes "[Adept Adventurer]";
			mes "This will open up the Status Window. Here you can change the pet's ^4d4fffname^000000 as well as check their ^4d4fffHunger^000000 and ^4d4fffIntimacy^000000.";
			next;
			mes "[Adept Adventurer]";
			mes "There are some special pets that gives special skills when their ^4d4fffIntimacy^000000 level becomes Loyal. Most pets start off as shy and time and food changes that.";
			next;
			break;
		case 4:
			mes "[Adept Adventurer]";
			mes "^4d4fff<Pet Food>^000000 is normal food for pets but some pets prefer other foods.";
			mes "You should keep enough with you so your pet doesn't get hungry.";
			next;
			mes "[Adept Adventurer]";
			mes "Pets will ^4d4fffrun away^000000 if they are too full or too hungry. So make sure you check your pets hunger status frequently!";
			if(getarg(0))
				mes "As long as they are out, they will continually decrease in intimacy, with some losing it faster than others.";
			next;
			break;
		case 5:
			mes "[Adept Adventurer]";
			if(getarg(0))
				mes "When very loyal, some pets will give special bonuses.";
			else
				mes "Some pets will give special bonuses when they are very loyal.";
			next;
			break;
		case 6:
			mes "[Adept Adventurer]";
			mes "Some pets can even wear accessory items.";
			mes "^4d4fff<Pet Groomer>^000000 will sell some pet accessory items but some monsters will also drop pet accessory items as well.";
			next;
			break;
		case 7:
			mes "[Adept Adventurer]";
			mes "I think it is better off experiencing more together than "+(getarg(0)?"just leaving them in the egg all the time.":"transforming back to the eggs?");
			next;
			break;
		case 8:
			mes "[Adept Adventurer]";
			mes "Come back again when you have another question.";
			close;
	}
	return;
}

OnTimer60000:
	stopnpctimer;
	set .@rnd,rand(1,4);
	if(.@rnd == 1)
		set .@talk$,"Adventurer's Pet : Red Potion.. Is it delicious? Herb does not look delicious.. I bet that is bitter.";
	else if(.@rnd == 2)
		set .@talk$,"Adventurer's Pet : Ha. You are lucky for having me.";
	else if(.@rnd == 3)
		set .@talk$,"Adventurer's Pet : Isn't the floor cold? Well.. For me.. Undead is more familiar.";
	else
		set .@talk$,"Adventurer's Pet : Yawn~ I am so bored!";
	npctalk .@talk$;
	//Fall through
OnInit:
	initnpctimer;
	end;
}

			warp "iz_ac02",84,79;
		else if(.@job$ == "Gunslinger")
			warp "iz_ac02",123,79;
		else if(.@job$ == "Ninja")
			warp "iz_ac02",123,139;
		end;
	} else {
		mes "[Cream Puff]";
		mes "Class aptitude test is nonsense for those who already have a job.";
		emotion e_sigh;
		close2;
		cutin "",255;
		end;
	}
}

								mes "[Lusa]";
								mes "Do ya have any other questions?";
								next;
								break;
							case 4:
								mes "[Lusa]";
								mes "If ya need more questions you can always come back ta me.";
								close2;
								cutin "",255;
								end;
						}
					}
				case 5:
					close2;
					cutin "",255;
					end;
			}
		} else {
			mes "[Lusa]";
			mes "Oh! I am sorry but in order to take the class, y'all have to register first. Ya come back here after registration at that counter there on the 1st floor, ya hear?";
			close2;
			cutin "",255;
			end;
		}
	} else if(Class == Job_Gunslinger) {
		if(BaseLevel < 21) {
			mes "[Lusa]";
			mes "Oh! Are you just darling, a newly minted gunslinger!";
			next;
			mes "[Lusa]";
			mes "Why your shootin iron looks shinier then a silver zeny! Do ya need anything?";
			next;
			if(select("Can you help me get to Einbroch?:No, thanks.") == 1) {
				mes "[Lusa]";
				mes "Sure, why not? Make sure to spend some time trainin!";
				next;
				mes "[Lusa]";
				mes "Get over there ya scamp!";
				close2;
				warp "que_ng",150,167;
				end;
			}
			mes "[Lusa]";
			mes "Oh, I am glad to hear that you are so strong!";
			close2;
			cutin "",255;
			end;
		}
		mes "[Lusa]";
		mes "Howdy! It's nice to see you again.";
		close2;
		cutin "",255;
		end;
	} else {
		mes "[Lusa]";
		mes "Hey! Y'all aren't gunslingers!";
		mes "Please leave!";
		close2;
		cutin "",255;
		end;
	}
}

							mes "[Mage Chuck]";
							mes "Try out the skills after equipping the^006400 Mage Manual^000000.";
							mes "Then hunt with the skills given to you in your skill window.";
							next;
							mes "[Mage Chuck]";
							mes "Anything else you want to know about Mages?";
							next;
							break;
						}
						if(!checkweight(1201,1) || (MaxWeight - Weight) < 2000) {
							mes "[Mage Chuck]";
							mes "If you want to become a Mage, lighten up your inventory load.";
							next;
							mes "[Mage Chuck]";
							mes "Anything else you want to know about Mages?";
							next;
							break;
						} else {
							mes "[Mage Chuck]";
							mes "Right, you must be set with your heart firm on becoming a Mage.";
							next;
							mes "[Mage Chuck]";
							mes "OK! Then I'll give you a chance to taste what it is to become a Mage.";
							mes "Take this ^007a02Mage Manual^000000.";
							mes "I'll let you borrow it!";
							next;
							mes "[Mage Chuck]";
							mes "Try out the skills after equipping the ^007a02Mage Manual^000000.";
							mes "Then hunt with the skills given to you in your skill window.";
							next;
							mes "[Mage Chuck]";
							mes "It's a valuable item so don't lose it.";
							mes "If you want to become a genius ^0000ffMage^000000 like me, follow in my path.";
							getitem 2824,1; //Mage_Manual
							close2;
							cutin "",255;
							end;
						}
					case 5:
						if(!callfunc("F_CanChangeJob")) {
							mes "[Mage Chuck]";
							mes "Oh, man your Basic Skill Level doesn't reach enough to be a Mge.";
							mes "Go back and level up your Basic Skill.";
							close2;
							cutin "",255;
							end;
						}
						mes "[Mage Chuck]";
						mes "Alright.. Sign the application form.... Wow~ You have a good handwriting! Ahh, okay. That's enough.";
						mes "You are... "+strcharinfo(0)+".";
						next;
						mes "[Mage Chuck]";
						mes "Hmm I can see that you've tried hard in your way. Though it seems to be a little clumsy, but well I think it's okay!";
						mes "Good! Always sticking to the basics is the best! I will transform you right away.";
						next;
						mes "[Mage Chuck]";
						mes "Hahh! You are now a Mage, one of our colleagues!";
						mes "We welcome you to the Mage Guild, our new friend!";
						next;
						mes "[Mage Chuck]";
						mes "'Welcome to the Mage Guild~'";
						mes "Congratulations on becoming a member of the Mage Guild! Go for it!";
						callfunc "Job_Change",Job_Mage;
						getitem 1639,1;	//N_Rod
						close2;
						cutin "",255;
						end;
					case 6:
						mes "[Mage Chuck]";
						mes "Yes~ Go meet other teachers then come back.";
						mes "Of course, Mages are most alluring of them all.~";
						next;
						mes "[Mage Chuck]";
						mes "You'll choose Mage again I have no doubt about it~~!!";
						mes "Haha see you later~";
						close2;
						cutin "",255;
						end;
				}
			}
		} else {
			mes "[Mage Chuck]";
			mes "First you'll have to complete your ^8b4513registration^000000 at the Academy front desk.";
			mes "If you go to the 1st floor of the academy someone will help you register.";
			close2;
			cutin "",255;
			end;
		}
	} else {
		mes "[Mage Chuck]";
		mes "You're no longer the innocent ^8b4513Novice^000000 who doesn't know anything~?";
		mes "I don't have anything to teach you~!";
		close2;
		cutin "",255;
		end;
	}
}

	if(!checkweight(1201,1) || (MaxWeight - Weight) < 2000) {
		mes "- Quest cannot be continued due to the overloaded inventory.";
		mes "- Please try it again after organizing the items.";
		close;
	}
	cutin "nov_lumin01",2;
	if(!isbegin_quest(7485)) {
		mes "[Lumin]";
		mes "The intoxicated enemies won't die only from poisoning.";
		mes "They only come close to death.";
		next;
		mes "[Lumin]";
		mes ".. Why do Porings turn their back?";
		close2;
		cutin "",255;
		end;
	} else {
		if(Class != Job_Novice) {
			mes "[Lumin]";
			mes "At last, the day comes.";
			next;
			mes "- Lumin changing clothes piece by piece.";
			cutin "",255;
			setnpcdisplay("Lumin#"+strnpcinfo(2),4_M_THIEF_RUMIN);
			specialeffect EF_SPHERE;
			specialeffect EF_SPHERE;
			next;
			cutin "thf_lumin01",2;
			mes "[Lumin]";
			mes "I was carrying out my mission.";
			next;
			select("No need to make an excuse....");
			cutin "thf_lumin05",2;
			mes "[Lumin]";
			mes "At least to you, I don't want to be a stranger.";
			mes "Forget what you saw today, as I have to introduce to the way of thief guild as many people as possible.";
			close2;
			cutin "",255;
			setnpcdisplay("Lumin#"+strnpcinfo(2),4_M_NOV_RUMIN);
			specialeffect EF_SPHERE;
			specialeffect EF_SPHERE;
			end;
		}
		if(checkquest(7487) == 2) {
			cutin "nov_lumin02",2;
			mes "[Lumin]";
			mes "We may meet again.";
			mes "Becoming familiar with others is pleasure and sad.";
			next;
			mes "[Lumin]";
			mes "... It may be in trouble if it dies upfront..";
			close2;
			cutin "",255;
			end;
		}
		if(!isbegin_quest(7487,HUNTING)) {
			mes "[Lumin]";
			mes "Your eagerness and efforts to complete mission moved me to offer something.";
			next;
			mes "[Lumin]";
			mes "^4d4fffIt is to hunt all 4 Porings here within 30 seconds^000000.";
			mes "If you do, I will yield to you all the earned item in my hand.";
			next;
			select("If fail?");
			mes "[Lumin]";
			mes "It is our bet. You have to give up yours as you lost.";
			mes "Emmm. As I am generous, I will recieve ^4d4fff10 Novice Red Potions^000000.";
			next;
			if(select("Give it up.:OK. I will accept this bet.") == 1) {
				cutin "nov_lumin02",2;
				mes "[Lumin]";
				mes ".... Eh...";
				mes "Coward.";
				close2;
				cutin "",255;
				end;
			}
			mes "[Lumin]";
			mes ".... Good!...";
			mes "Now, I am counting.";
			mes "^4d4fffSpeak to me once you finish 4 porings in 30 seconds^000000.";
			setquest 7487;
			close2;
			cutin "",255;
			end;
		} else if(!checkquest(7487,HUNTING)) {
			mes "[Lumin]";
			mes "You may be too busy in ^4d4fffhunting 4 porings in 30 seconds.^000000";
			mes "Hey, time passes now...";
			close2;
			cutin "",255;
			end;
		} else if(checkquest(7487,HUNTING) == 1) {
			mes "[Lumin]";
			mes "........... passed 30 seconds and have not hunted 4 porings yet.";
			mes "Then, it is not interesting.";
			next;
			mes "[Lumin]";
			mes "If you don't like do it... No way.";
			mes "As I am generous, I disregard the bet this time.";
			erasequest 7487;
			close2;
			cutin "",255;
			end;
		} else {
			if(checkquest(7487,PLAYTIME) == 2) {
				cutin "nov_lumin02",2;
				mes "[Lumin]";
				mes "Regretfully, 30 seconds has passed.";
				mes ".....";
				next;
				cutin "nov_lumin03",2;
				mes "[Lumin]";
				mes "I will give it to you.";
				mes "Fighting!!!";
				completequest 7487;
				getexp 800,50;
				getitem 512,22; //Apple
				next;
				select("Why are you treating me like this?:I lost?");
				cutin "nov_lumin05",2;
				mes "[Lumin]";
				mes "You spent time with me.";
				mes "Get it free. I stole them from Porings.";
			} else {
				cutin "nov_lumin03",2;
				mes "[Lumin]";
				mes "Oh, excellent!";
				mes "Now, I will give you the promised trophies.";
				next;
				cutin "nov_lumin05",2;
				mes "[Lumin]";
				mes "I had a fun thanks to you.";
				completequest 7487;
				getexp 800,50;
				getitem 512,3; //Apple
				getitem 511,2; //Green_Herb
				getitem 569,22; //Novice_Potion
				getitem 622,1; //Rainbow_Carrot
			}
			close2;
			cutin "",255;
			end;
		}
	}

OnInit:
	questinfo 7487,QTYPE_QUEST,0;
	setquestinfo_req 7487,7485,1;
	end;

iz_ac02_c,62,139,3	duplicate(LuminAcademy)	Lumin#2ac_c	4_M_NOV_RUMIN
iz_ac02_d,62,139,3	duplicate(LuminAcademy)	Lumin#2ac_d	4_M_NOV_RUMIN

-	script	tf_mobct#2ac	-1,{
	end;

OnMyMobDead:
	set .MyMobs,.MyMobs+1;
	if(.MyMobs == 4) {
		set .MyMobs,0;
		initnpctimer;
	}
	end;
OnTimer10000:
OnRespawn:
	setarray .@a[0],
		59,131,60,131,61,131,62,131;

	stopnpctimer;
	for(set .@i,0; .@i < getarraysize(.@a); set .@i,.@i+2) {
		monster "iz_ac02",.@a[.@i],.@a[.@i+1],"Poring",1725,1,"tf_mobct#2ac::OnMyMobDead";
		.GID = $@mobid[0];
		getunitdata .GID,.@temp;
		set .@temp[9],.@temp[9]^((MD_CANMOVE|MD_CANATTACK)&.@temp[9]);
		setunitdata .GID,9,.@temp[9];
		setunitdata .GID,31,1;
	}
	end;
OnInit:
	setcell "iz_ac02",59,131,62,131,cell_walkable,1;
	donpcevent "tf_mobct#2ac::OnRespawn";
	end;
}

OnRespawn:
	setarray .@a[0],
		59,143,60,143,61,143,62,143;

	stopnpctimer;
	for(set .@i,0; .@i < getarraysize(.@a); set .@i,.@i+2) {
		monster "iz_ac02_a",.@a[.@i],.@a[.@i+1],"Poring",1725,1,"3tf_mobct#2ac_a::OnMyMobDead";
		.GID = $@mobid[0];
		getunitdata .GID,.@temp;
		set .@temp[9],.@temp[9]^((MD_CANMOVE|MD_CANATTACK)&.@temp[9]);
		setunitdata .GID,9,.@temp[9];
		setunitdata .GID,31,1;
	}
	end;
OnInit:
	setcell "iz_ac02_a",59,143,62,143,cell_walkable,1;
	donpcevent "3tf_mobct#2ac_a::OnRespawn";
	end;
}

		mes "[Alcie Yisha]";
		mes "Did you ^ff0000register with the Criatura Academy^000000?";
		mes "You can register at ^ff0000information center of Criatura Academy^000000.";
		next;
		cutin "acact_01",2;
		mes "[Alcie Yisha]";
		mes "It is annoying.. but you need to register so you can recieve ^ff0000lots of education and service of Criatura Academy^000000.";
		close2;
		cutin "",255;
		end;
	}
}

-	script	::TrainingInstructor	4_F_03,{
	mes "[Training Instructor]";
	mes "The training grounds have been revised.";
	mes "I will send you to Izlude.";
	close2;
	erasequest 7117,7127;
	if(strnpcinfo(4) == "new_1-1" || strnpcinfo(4) == "new_1-2" || strnpcinfo(4) == "new_1-3" || strnpcinfo(4) == "new_1-4") {
		.@warp$ = "iz_int";
	} else if(strnpcinfo(4) == "new_2-1" || strnpcinfo(4) == "new_2-2" || strnpcinfo(4) == "new_2-3" || strnpcinfo(4) == "new_2-4") {
		.@warp$ = "iz_int01";
	} else if(strnpcinfo(4) == "new_3-1" || strnpcinfo(4) == "new_3-2" || strnpcinfo(4) == "new_3-3" || strnpcinfo(4) == "new_3-4") {
		.@warp$ = "iz_int02";
	} else if(strnpcinfo(4) == "new_4-1" || strnpcinfo(4) == "new_4-2" || strnpcinfo(4) == "new_4-3" || strnpcinfo(4) == "new_4-4") {
		.@warp$ = "iz_int03";

		.@warp$ = "iz_int04";
	}
	savepoint .@warp$,98,88;
	warp .@warp$,98,88;
	end;
}
